13      "source": [ 
14       "import math\n", 
15       "import zipfile\n", 
16       "\n", 
17       "from IPython.core.display import display\n", 
18       "from PIL import Image, ImageDraw, ImageFont\n", 
19       "import pytesseract\n", 
20       "import cv2 as cv\n", 
21       "import numpy as np\n", 
22       "\n", 
23       "# loading the face detection classifier\n", 
24       "face_cascade = cv.CascadeClassifier('readonly/haarcascade_frontalface_default.xml')\n", 
25       "\n", 
26       "# class declaration for storing photos, text on it, and pictures with faces\n", 
27       "class AnalyzedPhoto:\n", 
28       "\n", 
29       "    # A method that recognizes text in an image\n", 
30       "    # Used when initializing a class and stored in \".text\"\n", 
31       "    def text_on_photo(self):\n", 
32       "        changed_photo = self.pix.convert('L')\n", 
33       "        for x in range(changed_photo.width):\n", 
34       "            for y in range(changed_photo.height):\n", 
35       "                if changed_photo.getpixel((x,y)) > 245:\n", 
36       "                    changed_photo.putpixel((x,y), 255)\n", 
37       "                else:\n", 
38       "                    changed_photo.putpixel((x,y), 0)\n", 
39       "\n", 
40       "        return pytesseract.image_to_string(changed_photo)\n", 
41       "\n", 
42       "    # A method that recognizes faces in a picture and composes a single picture from them\n", 
43       "    # Used when initializing a class and stored in \".faces\"\n", 
44       "    def search_faces(self):\n", 
45       "        open_cv_photo = np.array(self.pix.convert(\"L\"))\n", 
46       "        faces_lst = face_cascade.detectMultiScale(open_cv_photo, 1.35)\n", 
47       "        if len(faces_lst) == 0:\n", 
48       "            self.faces = False\n", 
49       "            return False\n", 
50       "        max_width = 100\n", 
51       "        max_height = 100\n", 
52       "\n", 
53       "        faces_sheet = Image.new(self.pix.mode, (max_width * 5, max_height * math.ceil(len(faces_lst) / 5)))\n", 
54       "        x1=0\n", 
55       "        y1=0\n", 
56       "\n", 
57       "        for x,y,w,h in faces_lst:\n", 
58       "            face_photo = self.pix.crop((x,y,x+w,y+h))\n", 
59       "            face_photo.thumbnail((max_width, max_height))\n", 
60       "            faces_sheet.paste(face_photo, (x1, y1))\n", 
61       "            if x1+max_width == faces_sheet.width:\n", 
62       "                x1=0\n", 
63       "                y1=y1+max_height\n", 
64       "            else:\n", 
65       "                x1=x1+max_width\n", 
66       "\n", 
67       "\n", 
68       "        return faces_sheet\n", 
69       "\n", 
70       "\n", 
71       "    # Initializing the class\n", 
72       "    def __init__(self, p, ni):\n", 
73       "        self.pix = p                           #Photo for analysis\n", 
74       "        self.name = ni                         #Photo title\n", 
75       "        self.text = self.text_on_photo()       #Text on it\n", 
76       "        self.faces = self.search_faces()       #Picture with faces on it\n", 
77       "\n", 
78       "\n", 
79       "    def __str__(self):\n", 
80       "        return self.name\n", 
81       "\n", 
82       "    # Overriding the method from \"Display\", so that the class can handle \"Display\" and get a picture\n", 
83       "    def _repr_png_(self):\n", 
84       "        return display(self.pix)\n", 
85       "\n", 
86       "    # Overriding the method from \"Display\", so that the class can handle \"Display\"\n", 
87       "    # and not get a text\n", 
88       "    def __repr__(self):\n", 
89       "        return \"\"\n", 
90       "\n", 
91       "# Unpacking the archive into list of tuples (\"photo\", \"name of photo\")\n", 
92       "def unpack(file_name):\n", 
93       "    zip_file = zipfile.ZipFile(file_name, mode=\"r\")\n", 
94       "    photo_lst = []\n", 
95       "    for photo in zip_file.namelist():\n", 
96       "        photo_lst.append((Image.open(zip_file.open(photo)),photo))\n", 
97       "    zip_file.close()\n", 
98       "    return photo_lst\n", 
99       "\n", 
100      "\n", 
101      "\n", 
102      "\n" 
103     ]

127      "# Function for finding words in a picture and displaying faces from it\n", 
128      "def search_word(final_images_lst, word):\n", 
129      "    # See if there are words in a separate picture\n", 
130      "    images_with_word = {}\n", 
131      "    output_image_height = 0\n", 
132      "    for final_image in final_images_lst:\n", 
133      "        if word in final_image.text:\n", 
134      "            if final_image.faces:\n", 
135      "                images_with_word[final_image] = True\n", 
136      "                output_image_height += final_image.faces.height\n", 
137      "            else:\n", 
138      "                images_with_word[final_image] = False\n", 
139      "                output_image_height += 25\n", 
140      "            output_image_height += 25\n", 
141      "    # Create final picture\n", 
142      "    font1 = ImageFont.truetype(\"readonly/fanwood-webfont.ttf\", 20)\n", 
143      "    final_sheet = Image.new(final_images_lst[0].pix.mode, (500, output_image_height))\n", 
144      "    y=0\n", 
145      "    for image in images_with_word:\n", 
146      "        draw = ImageDraw.Draw(final_sheet)\n", 
147      "        draw.text((0,y),\"Result is found in file {}\".format(image.name), font = font1 )\n", 
148      "        y += 25\n", 
149      "        if images_with_word[image]:\n", 
150      "            final_sheet.paste(image.faces, (0, y))\n", 
151      "            y += image.faces.height\n", 
152      "        else:\n", 
153      "            draw = ImageDraw.Draw(final_sheet)\n", 
154      "            draw.text((0,y),\"But there were no faces in that file!\", font = font1 )\n", 
155      "            y += 25\n", 
156      "\n", 
157      "    display(final_sheet)\n", 
158      "\n", 
159      "\n", 
160      "images1 = unpack(\"small_img.zip\")\n", 
161      "final_images1 = [AnalyzedPhoto(x,y) for (x,y) in images1]\n", 
162      "search_word(final_images1, \"Christopher\")\n", 
163      "\n", 
164      "images2 = unpack(\"images.zip\")\n", 
165      "final_images2 = [AnalyzedPhoto(x,y) for (x,y) in images2]\n", 
166      "search_word(final_images2, \"Mark\")\n", 
167      "\n", 
168      "\n"
